.IPA-label-small{font-size:85%}.mw-parser-output .references .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .infobox .IPA-label-small,.mw-parser-output .navbox .IPA-label-small{font-size:100%}</style><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">Spanish pronunciation:</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="es-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">&#91;\xc9\xa1waj\xcb\x88na\xce\xb2o&#93;</a></span>, <link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1177148991"><span class="IPA-label IPA-label-small">locally</span> <span class="IPA nowrap" lang="es-Latn-fonipa"><a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/Spanish" title="Help:IPA/Spanish">&#91;waj\xcb\x88na\xce\xb2o&#93;</a></span>) is a <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_barrio-pueblo" title="Guaynabo barrio-pueblo">city</a>, <a href="/wiki/San_Juan_metropolitan_area" class="mw-redirect" title="San Juan metropolitan area">suburb</a> of <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a> and <a href="/wiki/Municipalities_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Municipalities of Puerto Rico">municipality</a> in the northern part of <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico" title="Puerto Rico">Puerto Rico</a>, located in the northern coast of the island, north of <a href="/wiki/Aguas_Buenas,_Puerto_Rico" title="Aguas Buenas, Puerto Rico">Aguas Buenas</a>, south of <a href="/wiki/Cata%C3%B1o,_Puerto_Rico" title="Cata\xc3\xb1o, Puerto Rico">Cata\xc3\xb1o</a>, east of <a href="/wiki/Bayam%C3%B3n,_Puerto_Rico" title="Bayam\xc3\xb3n, Puerto Rico">Bayam\xc3\xb3n</a>, and west of <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a>. Guaynabo is spread over 9 barrios and <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_barrio-pueblo" title="Guaynabo barrio-pueblo">Guaynabo Pueblo</a> (the downtown area and the administrative center of the suburb). Guaynabo is considered, along with its neighbors \xe2\x80\x93 San Juan and the municipalities of <a href="/wiki/Bayam%C3%B3n,_Puerto_Rico" title="Bayam\xc3\xb3n, Puerto Rico">Bayam\xc3\xb3n</a>, <a href="/wiki/Carolina,_Puerto_Rico" title="Carolina, Puerto Rico">Carolina</a>, <a href="/wiki/Cata%C3%B1o,_Puerto_Rico" title="Cata\xc3\xb1o, Puerto Rico">Cata\xc3\xb1o</a>, <a href="/wiki/Trujillo_Alto,_Puerto_Rico" title="Trujillo Alto, Puerto Rico">Trujillo Alto</a>, and <a href="/wiki/Toa_Baja,_Puerto_Rico" title="Toa Baja, Puerto Rico">Toa Baja</a> \xe2\x80\x93 to be part of the <a href="/wiki/San_Juan%E2%80%93Caguas%E2%80%93Guaynabo_metropolitan_area#San_Juan_metropolitan_area" title="San Juan\xe2\x80\x93Caguas\xe2\x80\x93Guaynabo metropolitan area">San Juan metropolitan area</a>. It is also part of the larger <a href="/wiki/San_Juan%E2%80%93Caguas%E2%80%93Guaynabo_metropolitan_area" title="San Juan\xe2\x80\x93Caguas\xe2\x80\x93Guaynabo metropolitan area">San Juan-Caguas-Guaynabo Metropolitan Statistical Area</a>, (the largest <a href="/wiki/List_of_metropolitan_areas_of_the_United_States" class="mw-redirect" title="List of metropolitan areas of the United States">MSA</a> in Puerto Rico).\n</p><p>The municipality has a land area of 27.13 square miles (70.3&#160;km<sup>2</sup>) and a population of 89,780 as of the <a href="/wiki/2020_United_States_census" title="2020 United States census">2020 census</a>. The municipality is known for being an affluent suburb of San Juan and for its former <a href="/wiki/Irish_immigration_to_Puerto_Rico" title="Irish immigration to Puerto Rico">Irish</a> heritage. The studios of <a href="/wiki/WAPA-TV" title="WAPA-TV">WAPA-TV</a> is located in Guaynabo.\n</p>\n<meta property="mw:PageProp/toc" />\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="History">History</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" title="Edit section: History"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The first European settlement in Puerto Rico, <a href="/wiki/Caparra_Archaeological_Site" title="Caparra Archaeological Site">Caparra</a>, was founded in 1508 by <a href="/wiki/Juan_Ponce_de_Le%C3%B3n" title="Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n">Juan Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n</a> in land that is today part of Guaynabo. Ponce de Le\xc3\xb3n resided there as first Spanish governor of Puerto Rico. This settlement was abandoned in 1521 in favor of <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a>. The ruins of Caparra remain and are a U.S. <a href="/wiki/National_Historic_Landmark" title="National Historic Landmark">National Historic Landmark</a>. The Museum of the Conquest and Colonization of Puerto Rico, which features artifacts from the site and others in Puerto Rico, is located on the grounds.\n</p><p>The municipality of Guaynabo was founded in 1769 by Pedro R. Davila (P.R.), after a struggle for division from the municipality of <a href="/wiki/Bayam%C3%B3n" class="mw-redirect" title="Bayam\xc3\xb3n">Bayam\xc3\xb3n</a>. Previously, the municipality was known as <b>Buinabo</b>, a name that it is popularly said to mean in <a href="/wiki/Ta%C3%ADno_language" title="Ta\xc3\xadno language">Ta\xc3\xadno</a> "<i>Here is another place of fresh water.</i>" Irish officer Thomas O\'Daly and fellow Irishman Miguel Kirwan settled the area in the late 18th century and developed a farm and sugarcane plantation he named <b>Hacienda <a href="/wiki/Saint_Patrick" title="Saint Patrick">San Patricio</a></b>. The plantation no longer exists but the land on which it was located is now the central business district of Guaynabo and the <a href="/wiki/San_Patricio_Plaza" title="San Patricio Plaza">San Patricio Plaza</a> shopping mall.\n</p><p>On September 20, 2017 <a href="/wiki/Hurricane_Maria" title="Hurricane Maria">Hurricane Maria</a> struck Puerto Rico.  In Guaynabo, where 26.9% of the population live below the poverty level, 2800 homes were destroyed.<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-2"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>2<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> The hurricane triggered numerous landslides in Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-USGS_Maria_Landslides_3-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-USGS_Maria_Landslides-3"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>3<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-USGS_Maria_Landslides_map_4-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-USGS_Maria_Landslides_map-4"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>4<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Then president <a href="/wiki/Donald_Trump" title="Donald Trump">Donald Trump</a> and his wife, Melania Trump visited Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-NPR.org_2017_5-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-NPR.org_2017-5"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>5<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Due to the municipality\'s fiscal difficulties, it was not until April 2, 2019, over a year and half later, that the overtime pay owed to municipal workers was paid.<sup id="cite_ref-6" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-6"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>6<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>After 24 years as mayor, <a href="/wiki/H%C3%A9ctor_O%27Neill_Garc%C3%ADa" class="mw-redirect" title="H\xc3\xa9ctor O&#39;Neill Garc\xc3\xada">H\xc3\xa9ctor O\'Neill Garc\xc3\xada</a> resigned in 2017 when allegations surfaced of sexual harassment toward a female municipal employee.<sup id="cite_ref-7" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-7"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>7<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> He was replaced in a run-off election by <a href="/wiki/Angel_P%C3%A9rez_Otero" title="Angel P\xc3\xa9rez Otero">Angel P\xc3\xa9rez Otero</a>, who in turn was forced out due to his arrest for Federal corruption allegations in 2021.<sup id="cite_ref-8" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-8"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>8<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> H\xc3\xa9ctor O\'Neill\'s son Edward O\'Neill Rosa won the following run-off election to succeed him as mayor in January 2022.<sup id="cite_ref-9" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-9"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>9<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Geography">Geography</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Geography"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Guaynabo is on the northern side.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_10-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Barrios">Barrios</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Barrios"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<figure class="mw-halign-left" typeof="mw:File"><a href="/wiki/File:Barrios_of_Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg" class="mw-file-description" title="Barrios of Guaynabo, Puerto Rico locator map"><img alt="Barrios of Guaynabo, Puerto Rico locator map" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg/150px-Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg" decoding="async" width="150" height="333" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg/225px-Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/47/Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg/300px-Barrios_of_Guaynabo%2C_Puerto_Rico_locator_map.jpg 2x" data-file-width="1516" data-file-height="3370" /></a><figcaption>Barrios of Guaynabo, Puerto Rico locator map</figcaption></figure>\n<p>Like all municipalities of Puerto Rico, Guaynabo is subdivided into <a href="/wiki/Barrios_of_Puerto_Rico" title="Barrios of Puerto Rico">barrios</a>. The municipal buildings, central square and large Catholic church are located in a smaller barrio referred to as <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">"el pueblo"</i></span>, located near the center of the municipality.<sup id="cite_ref-Pico_1969_11-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Pico_1969-11"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>11<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Law2015_12-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Law2015-12"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>12<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-US2010Census_13-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-US2010Census-13"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>13<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-14" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-14"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>14<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1184024115">.mw-parser-output .div-col{margin-top:0.3em;column-width:30em}.mw-parser-output data-file-height="2500" /></a><figcaption>Guaynabo\'s town square in Guaynabo barrio-pueblo</figcaption></figure>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Sectors">Sectors</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="Edit section: Sectors"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r1236090951">.mw-parser-output .hatnote{font-style:italic}.mw-parser-output div.hatnote{padding-left:1.6em;margin-bottom:0.5em}.mw-parser-output .hatnote i{font-style:normal}.mw-parser-output .hatnote+link+.hatnote{margin-top:-0.5em}@media print{body.ns-0 .mw-parser-output .hatnote{display:none!important}}</style><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">Further information: <a href="/wiki/List_of_barrios_and_sectors_of_Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico" title="List of barrios and sectors of Guaynabo, Puerto Rico">List of barrios and sectors of Guaynabo, Puerto Rico</a></div>\n<p>Barrios (which are, in contemporary times, roughly comparable to <a href="/wiki/Minor_civil_divisions" class="mw-redirect" title="Minor civil divisions">minor civil divisions</a>)<sup id="cite_ref-Barrio-Pueblo_15-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Barrio-Pueblo-15"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>15<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> are further subdivided into smaller areas called <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">sectores</i></span>  (<i>sectors</i> in English). The types of <i>sectores</i> may vary, from normally <i>sector</i> to <i>urbanizaci\xc3\xb3n</i> to <i>reparto</i> to <i>barriada</i> to <i>residencial</i>, among others.<sup id="cite_ref-16" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-16"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>16<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-17" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-17"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>17<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-Law_1-2001_18-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-Law_1-2001-18"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>18<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Special_Communities">Special Communities</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Special Communities"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<link rel="mw-deduplicated-inline-style" href="mw-data:TemplateStyles:r1236090951"><div role="note" class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable">See also: <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Office_for_Socioeconomic_and_Community_Development" title="Puerto Rico Office for Socioeconomic and Community Development">Puerto Rico Office for Socioeconomic and Community Development</a></div>\n<p><span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Comunidades Especiales de Puerto Rico</i></span> (Special Communities of Puerto Rico) are marginalized communities whose citizens are experiencing a certain amount of <a href="/wiki/Social_exclusion" title="Social exclusion">social exclusion</a>. A map shows these communities occur in nearly every municipality of the commonwealth. Of the 742 places that were on the list in 2014, the following barrios, communities, sectors, or neighborhoods were in Guaynabo: Amelia, Buen Samaritano, <a href="/wiki/Camarones,_Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Camarones, Guaynabo, Puerto Rico">Camarones</a> barrio, Corea, El Polvor\xc3\xadn, Honduras, Jerusal\xc3\xa9n, Los Filtros, Sector El Laberinto, Sector La Pajilla, Sector Los Ratones (Camino Feliciano), Sector San Miguel, Trujillo, Sector Tom\xc3\xa9, Vietnam,<sup id="cite_ref-19" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-19"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>19<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and Villa Isle\xc3\xb1a.<sup id="cite_ref-wordpress.com_20-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-wordpress.com-20"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>20<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-21" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-21"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>21<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Demographics">Demographics</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup></td></tr>\n</tbody></table>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Tourism">Tourism</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Tourism"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>To stimulate local tourism, the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Tourism_Company" title="Puerto Rico Tourism Company">Puerto Rico Tourism Company</a> launched the <i>Voy Turistiendo</i> ("I\'m Touring") campaign, with a passport book and website. The Guaynabo page lists <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Ruinas de Caparra</i></span>, <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Paseo Tablado</i></span>, and <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Plaza de Los Artistas</i></span>, as places of interest.<sup id="cite_ref-28" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-28"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>28<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Landmarks_and_places_of_interest">Landmarks and places of Buchanan</a></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Economy">Economy</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Economy"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Several businesses have their headquarters or local Puerto Rican branches in Guaynabo. <a href="/wiki/El_Nuevo_D%C3%ADa" title="El Nuevo D\xc3\xada">El Nuevo D\xc3\xada</a>,<sup id="cite_ref-30" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-30"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>30<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> <a href="/wiki/Chrysler" title="Chrysler">Chrysler</a>, <a href="/wiki/Santander_Group" class="mw-redirect" title="Santander Group">Santander</a> Securities, <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Telephone" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Telephone">Puerto Rico Telephone</a>, and many sales offices for large US and international firms (such as <a href="/wiki/Total_S.A." class="mw-redirect" title="Total S.A.">Total</a>, <a href="/wiki/Microsoft" title="Microsoft">Microsoft</a>, <a href="/wiki/Toshiba" title="Toshiba">Toshiba</a>, <a href="/wiki/Puma_Energy" title="Puma Energy">Puma Energy</a> and others) have their Puerto Rican headquarters in Guaynabo. <a href="/wiki/WAPA-TV" title="WAPA-TV">WAPA-TV</a> (Televicentro) and <a href="/wiki/Univision" title="Univision">Univision</a> Puerto Rico have their main studios in Guaynabo.\n</p><p><a href="/wiki/Iberia_Airlines" class="mw-redirect" title="Iberia Airlines">Iberia</a>\'s <a href="/wiki/San_Juan,_Puerto_Rico" title="San Juan, Puerto Rico">San Juan</a>-area offices are in Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-31" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-31"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>31<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Crime">Crime</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Crime"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Carjackings" class="mw-redirect" title="Carjackings">Carjackings</a> have been an ongoing problem in Guaynabo, Puerto Rico<sup id="cite_ref-32" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-32"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>32<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-33" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-33"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>33<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-34" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-34"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>34<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-35" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-35"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>35<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-36" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-36"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>36<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> and in 2014 the FBI reported a carjacking that occurred in <a href="/wiki/Camarones,_Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico" title="Camarones, Guaynabo, Puerto Rico">Camarones</a>.<sup id="cite_ref-37" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-37"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>37<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</td></tr></tbody></table>\n</div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Culture">Culture</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Culture"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Festivals_and_events">Festivals and events</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Festivals and events"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Guaynabo celebrates its <a href="/wiki/Fiestas_patronales_in_Puerto_Rico" title="Fiestas patronales in Puerto Rico">patron saint</a> festival in April. The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">Fiestas Patronales de San Pedro Martir</i></span> is a religious and cultural celebration that generally features parades, games, artisans, amusement rides, regional food, and live entertainment.<sup id="cite_ref-PR_Ency_10-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-PR_Ency-10"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>10<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-J.D._2006_39-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-J.D._2006-39"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>39<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Other festivals and events celebrated in Guaynabo include:\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Epiphany_(holiday)" title="Epiphany (holiday)">Three Kings</a> Festival \xe2\x80\x93 January</li>\n<li>Mab\xc3\xb3 Carnival \xe2\x80\x93 February</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Mother%27s_Day_(United_States)" title="Mother&#39;s Day (United States)">Mothers\xe2\x80\x99 Day</a> celebration \xe2\x80\x93 May</li>\n<li>National <a href="/wiki/Salsa_music" title="Salsa music">Salsa</a> Day \xe2\x80\x93 June</li>\n<li>Fine Arts camp and recreation and sports camp \xe2\x80\x93 June</li>\n<li>Bomba and Plena (folkloric music and dance) Festival \xe2\x80\x93 October</li>\n<li>Official lighting of <a href="/wiki/Christmas" title="Christmas">Christmas</a> Lights \xe2\x80\x93 November</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Sports">Sports</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Sports"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Guaynabo\'s old <a href="/wiki/National_Superior_Basketball_League_of_Puerto_Rico" class="mw-redirect" title="National Superior Basketball League of Puerto Rico">BSN</a> team, the <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Mets" class="mw-redirect" title="Guaynabo Mets">Guaynabo Mets</a>, won national championships in 1980, 1982 and 1989, commanded by the player whom the <a href="/wiki/Mario_Morales_Coliseum" title="Mario Morales Coliseum">Mario Morales Coliseum</a> was named after, <a href="/wiki/Mario_Morales" title="Mario Morales">Mario "Quijote" Morales</a>. The Conquistadores de Guaynabo, or <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Conquistadores" class="mw-redirect" title="Guaynabo Conquistadores">Guaynabo Conquistadores</a>, are the <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Mets" class="mw-redirect" title="Guaynabo Mets">Guaynabo Mets</a> replacement and still play in the <a href="/wiki/Mario_Morales_Coliseum" title="Mario Morales Coliseum">Mario Morales Coliseum</a>. The <a href="/wiki/Mets_de_Guaynabo_(women%27s_volleyball)" title="Mets de Guaynabo (women&#39;s volleyball)">Mets de Guaynabo</a> are the local women\'s volleyball team that play in the <a href="/wiki/Liga_de_Voleibol_Superior_Femenino" title="Liga de Voleibol Superior Femenino">Liga de Voleibol Superior Femenino</a> (LVSF), winning three titles in 1978, 1993\xe2\x80\x9394 and 1995. They also play in the <a href="/wiki/Mario_Morales_Coliseum" title="Mario Morales Coliseum">Mario Morales Coliseum</a>. <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Fluminense_FC" title="Guaynabo Fluminense FC">Guaynabo Fluminense FC</a> is Guaynabo\'s professional soccer team that plays in the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Soccer_League" title="Puerto Rico Soccer League">Puerto Rico Soccer League</a>. The league started in 2008 and Guaynabo\'s current position in the league is 4th place. <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Fluminense_FC" title="Guaynabo Fluminense FC">Guaynabo Fluminense FC</a> play their matches at the Jose Bonano Stadium that was originally made for baseball, but became a soccer arena after the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Baseball_League" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Baseball League">Puerto Rico Baseball League</a> was cancelled for the 2008 season. It was at the same year that the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Soccer_League" title="Puerto Rico Soccer League">Puerto Rico Soccer League</a> was starting to take place. In the 2009 season, <a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Fluminense_FC" title="Guaynabo Fluminense FC">Guaynabo Fluminense FC</a> moved to the <a href="/wiki/Estadio_Sixto_Escobar" title="Estadio Sixto Escobar">Sixto Escobar Stadium</a>.\n</p>\n<ul><li><a href="/wiki/Mets_de_Guaynabo_(women%27s_volleyball)" title="Mets de Guaynabo (women&#39;s volleyball)">Mets de Guaynabo</a> (women\'s volleyball) - <a href="/wiki/Liga_de_Voleibol_Superior_Femenino" title="Liga de Voleibol Superior Femenino">Liga de Voleibol Superior Femenino</a> (LVSF)</li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Mets_de_Guaynabo_(men%27s_volleyball)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Mets de Guaynabo (men&#39;s volleyball) (page does not exist)">Mets de Guaynabo</a> (men\'s volleyball) - <a href="/wiki/Liga_de_Voleibol_Superior_Masculino" title="Liga de Voleibol Superior Masculino">Liga de Voleibol Superior Masculino</a> (LVSM)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Conquistadores" class="mw-redirect" title="Guaynabo Conquistadores">Guaynabo Conquistadores</a> (basketball) - <a href="/wiki/Baloncesto_Superior_Nacional" title="Baloncesto Superior Nacional">Baloncesto Superior Nacional</a> (BSN)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Mets" class="mw-redirect" title="Guaynabo Mets">Mets de Guaynabo</a> (basketball) - <a href="/wiki/Baloncesto_Superior_Nacional" title="Baloncesto Superior Nacional">Baloncesto Superior Nacional</a> (BSN)</li>\n<li><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo_Mets_(baseball)&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" class="new" title="Guaynabo Mets (baseball) (page does not exist)">Mets de Guaynabo</a> (baseball) - <a href="/wiki/Federaci%C3%B3n_de_B%C3%A9isbol_Aficionado_de_Puerto_Rico" title="Federaci\xc3\xb3n de B\xc3\xa9isbol Aficionado de Puerto Rico">Federaci\xc3\xb3n de B\xc3\xa9isbol Aficionado de Puerto Rico</a> (B\xc3\xa9isbol Doble A)</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Guaynabo_Fluminense_FC" title="Guaynabo Fluminense FC">Guaynabo Fluminense FC</a> (soccer) - <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Soccer_League" title="Puerto Rico Soccer League">Puerto Rico Soccer League</a> (PRSL)</li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Government_and_infrastructure">Government and infrastructure</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Government and infrastructure"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/United_States_Postal_Service" title="United States Postal Service">United States Postal Service</a> operates two post offices, Guaynabo and Caparra Heights, in Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-40" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-40"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>40<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-41" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-41"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>41<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>The <a href="/wiki/Federal_Bureau_of_Prisons" title="Federal Bureau of Prisons">Federal Bureau of Prisons</a> operates the <a href="/wiki/Metropolitan_Detention_Center,_Guaynabo" title="Metropolitan Detention Center, Guaynabo">Metropolitan Detention Center, Guaynabo</a> in Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-42" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-42"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>42<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p><p>Some regions of the city belong to the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Senatorial_district_I" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Senatorial district I">Puerto Rico Senatorial district I</a> while others belong to the <a href="/wiki/Puerto_Rico_Senatorial_district_II" class="mw-redirect" title="Puerto Rico Senatorial district II">Puerto Rico Senatorial district II</a>. Both of the Districts are represented by two Senators. In 2016, <a href="/wiki/Henry_Neumann" title="Henry Neumann">Henry Neumann</a> and <a href="/wiki/Miguel_Romero" title="Miguel Romero">Miguel Romero</a> were elected as Senators for District I, while <a href="/wiki/Migdalia_Padilla" title="Migdalia Padilla">Migdalia Padilla</a> and <a href="/wiki/Carmelo_R%C3%ADos_Santiago" title="Carmelo R\xc3\xados Santiago">Carmelo R\xc3\xados</a> have been serving as Senators for District II since being elected in 2004.<sup id="cite_ref-43" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-43"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>43<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Mayors">Mayors</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Symbols">Symbols</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Symbols"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <span title="Spanish-language text"><i lang="es">municipio</i></span> has an official flag and coat of arms.<sup id="cite_ref-44" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-44"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>44<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Flag">Flag</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: Flag"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>This municipality has a flag.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_45-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-45"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>45<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading3"><h3 id="Coat_of_arms">Coat of arms</h3><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Coat of arms"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>This municipality has a coat of arms.<sup id="cite_ref-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020_45-1" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-LexJuris_(Leyes_y_Jurisprudencia)_de_Puerto_Rico_2020-45"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>45<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Health_facilities">Health facilities</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Health facilities"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p><a href="/wiki/Professional_Hospital_Guaynabo" title="Professional Hospital Guaynabo">Professional Hospital Guaynabo</a> located on Felisa Rinc\xc3\xb3n Avenue (formerly Las Cumbres Avenue), is the newest hospital infrastructure built in Puerto Rico. Guaynabo is the only city in Puerto Rico to have a hospital specialized in advanced vascular surgery.<sup id="cite_ref-46" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-46"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>46<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup> Some of the first and newest procedures performed in Puerto Rico during 2009 were done in Professional Hospital Guaynabo, including the first AxiaLIF surgery for <a href="/wiki/Lumbar" title="Lumbar">lumbar</a> fusion.<sup id="cite_ref-47" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-47"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>47<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Transportation">Transportation</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Transportation"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>The <a href="/wiki/Tren_Urbano" title="Tren Urbano">Tren Urbano</a> has only one station in the municipality, <a href="/wiki/Torrimar_station" title="Torrimar station">Torrimar Station</a>.\nGuaynabo has a bus network called \xe2\x80\x9cGuaynabo City Transport\xe2\x80\x9d.\nThere are 63 bridges in Guaynabo.<sup id="cite_ref-bridge_48-0" class="reference"><a href="#cite_note-bridge-48"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>48<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="Notable_people">Notable people</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a player who played most for the <a href="/wiki/Cincinnati_Reds" title="Cincinnati Reds">Cincinnati Reds</a></li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Carlos_Mel%C3%A9ndez_(singer)" title="Carlos Mel\xc3\xa9ndez (singer)">Carlos</a> (born 1965), <a href="/wiki/%C3%93scar_Mel%C3%A9ndez" title="\xc3\x93scar Mel\xc3\xa9ndez">Oscar</a> (born 1966), and <a href="/wiki/Ricky_Mel%C3%A9ndez" title="Ricky Nido">Tomas Nido</a> (born 1994), baseball catcher for the <a href="/wiki/New_York_Mets" title="New York Mets">New York Mets</a></li></ul>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 href="#cite_note-Doha-50"><span class="cite-bracket">&#91;</span>50<span class="cite-bracket">&#93;</span></a></sup>\n</p>\n<div class="mw-heading mw-heading2"><h2 id="International_relations">International relations</h2><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=Guaynabo,_Puerto_Rico&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: International relations"><span>edit</span></a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></div>\n<p>Guaynabo serves as a host city to four foreign consulates with business in Puerto Rico:\n</p>\n<ul><li><span data-sort-value="El Salvador"><span class="flagicon"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt="" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/23px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png" decoding="async" width="23" height="13" class="mw-file-element" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/35px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/34/Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg/46px-Flag_of_El_Salvador.svg.png 2x" data-file-width="1005" data-file-height="567" /></span></span>&#160;</span><a href="/wiki/El_Salvador" title="El Salvador">El Salvador</a></span></li>\n<li><span data-sort-value="Finland"><span class="flagicon"><span class="mw-image-border" typeof="mw:File"><span><img alt=""
